### AAS-055: Mimic's Mission: Build plugin for mockery/mockery
- **Description**: Friendly Request: Can I build a plugin for 'mockery/mockery'?

Context: Mockery is a simple yet flexible PHP mock object framework for use in unit testing with PHPUnit, PHPSpec or any other testing framework. Its core goal is to offer a test double framework with a succinct API capable of clearly defining all possible object operations and interactions using a human readable Domain Specific Language (DSL).
Source: https://github.com/mockery/mockery

This was harvested during a Mimic's Mission as a potential shortcut for Guild quests.
- **Status**: PENDING APPROVAL (User must change to 'queued' to start)

### AAS-056: Mimic's Mission: Build plugin for AutoFixture/AutoFixture
- **Description**: Friendly Request: Can I build a plugin for 'AutoFixture/AutoFixture'?

Context: AutoFixture is an open source library for .NET designed to minimize the 'Arrange' phase of your unit tests in order to maximize maintainability. Its primary goal is to allow developers to focus on what is being tested rather than how to setup the test scenario, by making it easier to create object graphs containing test data.
Source: https://github.com/AutoFixture/AutoFixture

### AAS-060: Mimic's Mission: Build plugin for prateek147/DVIA
- **Description**: Friendly Request: Can I build a plugin for 'prateek147/DVIA'?

Context: Damn Vulnerable iOS App (DVIA) is an iOS application that is damn vulnerable. Its main goal is to provide a platform to mobile security enthusiasts/professionals or students to test their iOS penetration testing skills in a legal environment. This application covers all the common vulnerabilities found in iOS applications (following OWASP top 10 mobile risks) and contains several challenges that the user can try. This application also contains a section where a user can read various articles on iOS application security. This project is developed and maintained by @prateekg147. The vulnerabilities and solutions covered in this app are tested upto iOS 8.1 . 
Source: https://github.com/prateek147/DVIA
